Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when all the pus that is in the abscess has been drained, apply clean cotton to the wound and leave it until the next day; then remove the cotton and treat with an appropriate ointment until it heals.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscesses are like scrofula, they should be treated as we have said for scrofula fissures, and if the wound is closed, a cautery should be administered as mentioned earlier.
de la routure de l’artere	of the rupture of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme; et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont; et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement; et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans; et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	When the artery is swollen and the skin above it, this often causes abscesses, and the same happens to the vein, which becomes swollen and abscessed; and one can tell the cause is the artery when the abscess is long and deep; and when you touch it with your fingers, you feel a tugging; and when the cause is the vein, there are red spots apparent; and it is foolish to cover this kind of abscess, especially when it is under the armpits or around the anus, neck, or in many other places, and it is very serious.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc; puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte; puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples; puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme; puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient; puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit; puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil; et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus; puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez; puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore one must avoid cauterizing with iron, and also cut the one on top if it is due to a swollen artery; then open the vein at its base, and carefully separate the artery from the veins, so that it is exposed; then insert a needle underneath where there is an artery, and have it pierce through to the other side, and tie the artery with a double thread in two places according to how I taught you for the extraction of the two arteries in the temples; then stab the place between the two threads with an instrument, so that the blood within comes out which is causing the abscess; then administer the cautery which bends a bow, until the ligature comes undone; then treat it with ointment suitable to it, until it is healed; and if the abscess is due to opening a vein, then one must dye their hand with the pus from the abscess all over the skin, then insert another needle underneath where they are holding the hand, have it pierce through, and tie a double thread around it in three places; then lance the abscess so that the excess comes out, then lance the skin and leave what is tied; then place a moistened cloth in wine and oil on top of it, then administer treatments with poultices and ointments until it is healed.
des apostemes des ners	of abscesses of the nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Also, as abscesses come in the artery and vein, so do they come to the nerves when they are hurt, or from too great exertion, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor; et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur; et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer: par aventure i vanroit contraction; et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	And this happens most often in the shoulders and elbows and in all places where there are joints, and it is a grievous abscess, and its color resembles the color of the body, and it is in various dispositions without pain; and when one presses it firmly, the patient feels pain, and it is not at the surface of the body but deep within; and it becomes numb in all parts, and it cannot go forward or backward, or downward or upward, and that which is in joints should not be covered with iron: for there might be contraction; and that which is on the head or forehead, treat with a poultice.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine; et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the abscess is small, hold it with tweezers and pull out the root; if it is large, cut it open at the base, then scrape it, then remove the bone, and close the wound with stitches, then heal it completely.
des grosses boces pendans	of large dangling
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros; et en i a de petis et de mout grans; et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	There is a disease that sometimes affects the stomach and no other part; it is called "fungus" because of its resemblance to ears, having thin roots and thick stems. There are both small and very large ones. I saw a man who had two on his stomach that looked more like fungi than anything else, without any difference, white in color, with slender roots, and split open, from which moisture would leak out.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine; si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	I cut them out and found one weighing 18 ounces and the other 6 ounces; their treatment is to incise and look if the disease is moist, and the color of the skin is white and moist with slender roots. Then cut with a wide spatula and apply fire cautery in your presence.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer; et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors; et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail; et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne; puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	For when cutting, there are often large blood vessels that need to be cauterized immediately, and if the patient is frightened of the incision with the iron, take a well-prepared piece of linen thread and tie it around the skin as described, and leave it for two days; then tie it tightly, and do not stop tightening the thread until the skin is cut through, and if the roots are large, one must be cautious about cutting in the same way for the stomach, but you can certainly cut half of it, then cauterize it so that it does not return, then treat the wound and take care not to cut into the skin that is a pale color and has poor sensation and looks like milk.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is an encrusted abscess, and I will come to the treatment of ulcers next.
quant li boude ist fuer	when the boil has broken
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit; et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	If the appearance of the boil comes from cautery on a wound or from a fissure in the syphilitic sore, and it is on the belly and in some of the bowels, as happens in other roux, or from blood that flows from veins or arteries according to what is before, or from flatulence; and if it is by the roux of the syphilitic sore and by the discharge of the bowel, then the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the body, and it is a slight thing without pain, and there are various discharges.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is due to the protrusion of the intestine, then it is more diverse, and when pressed by hand it springs back, and sometimes it retreats, and if constricted, it grows larger at the entrance of the bath and from great exertion.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie; et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit; et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	And if it is due to moisture, it is a slight thing, and it opens easily when you press it with your hand, and it does not constrict; and if it is due to blood, then the abscesses are large and hard, and they are fixed according to a quantity; and if it is due to flatulence, then it is soft to the touch, and the action is that you should look to see whether the appearance is due to blood from an artery or vein, or flatulence.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	If you must let the wound heal.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear, as I have told you in the chapter on abscesses, because of the artery and vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude; puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine; puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz; puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine; se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre; et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit; et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier; puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi; ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit; et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	And if the appearance is in the intestine or bowels, then you must command the patient to tighten his belt and be stretched out straight, then sign all around the swollen area; then command him to lie still between your hands, then go around the area that you have marked all around the spasm, then extend half of the abscess upwards to the large knuckle; then tie it tightly around with a strong thread or a strong silk cord, and let the patient's nose be free; then open half of the abscess over the string, and put your finger inside, and feel for the intestine; if you find it caught in the string, then release it, and pull out the intestine from the abdomen; and if you find the bowels, grab them at the knuckle and cut off the excess; and if the artery or vein makes a noise, walk gently all around, then return to your work and take two needles, and put two strong threads through them, and pierce what you have made in the form of a cross; then pull out the abscess in four places on the needles, and if you see any, remove the needles, and let the place heal as it can, and cut away the dead flesh by itself; or when it becomes subtle and heals, then cure it as appropriate, and draw out the blood or moisture that you find, then cure the wound appropriately, and close up the wound.
dou chancre	from sores [ulcers]
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer; et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement; et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner; ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	We have discussed the different types of sores [ulcers] and how to treat them with medication, including the use of cauterization with iron. We have also mentioned sores that appear in the mouth, and how to care for them. The ancients say that when sores are in places where they can be reached, such as in the breasts or thighs, and similar areas, they should be removed completely when they are new. However, once they become large and old, one should not touch them, as I have never seen anyone heal from them; nor has anyone healed from them before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire; puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide .i. boin leu por faire l’ovraige; puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier; et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the work, when it is in place where it can be removed, as we have said, is that you sometimes purge the patient of black bile; then make him bleed if he has a manifest fullness, then prepare the patient .i. good site for the operation; then cut your onchites or ulcer, and the hair all over, and the bone all over without leaving anything; and let the blood run out completely, and express the site well with your hand or something, and if the bleeding from the incision of the artery or vein makes you feel contrary, cauterize it until the blood vessels are stunned; then cure it with another cure until it is healed.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer: si est eclites soulement; et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances: c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose; donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses; si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance; et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer: lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	We have already described in the section on diagnosis the appearances of dropsy, how the accumulation of fluid occurs, the signs of each type, and the treatment using medication or iron. Only two types, tympanites and hydrops, should be treated with iron; these are deadly conditions. So, when treating a case of dropsy called 'eclites' with medication, and the treatment is ineffective, consider whether the patient is weak, or suffering from another ailment besides dropsy, such as stomach issues and similar conditions; in which case, do not use iron, as there is a risk involved. But if the patient is strong, and suffering only from dropsy, and neither too young nor too old, then proceed as follows: support the patient upright in your arms, and press on the abdomen to force the fluid down to the lowest part of the feet. Then, take the spiny spatula and insert it according to this procedure:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let there be two parts of a trenchant.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier; puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines: si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil; et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois; et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu; puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor; puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	And it should be pointed at both ends, but not so sharp that it can pierce the intestines when inserted, nor can it blister; then look to see if the dropsy is in the intestines. If it is due to liver disease, the incision should be on the left side of the navel; and if it is due to the spleen, it should be on the right. It is not good for the patient to lie on the incision so that the excess fluids do not flow into the weak area; then pierce all the way through the skin with the instrument, and squeeze out the fluid, and lift your hand slightly above the spatumile between the skin and the syphon as though skinning it to the thickness of a fingernail or nail clippings. Then pierce the syphon until the fluid comes out at the desired location; that is where the water is located. Then draw it out, and insert this instrument from which the fluid will be withdrawn.
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus; et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus; et II d’autre part, et I d’autre; et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	And it is similar to a silver cane, and is made of lightweight bronze or brass, and has a small hole in the lower part; and on one side there are three holes, and two on the other, and one on the other; and the head is cut like a feather, and this is the shape of the incision that scribes make when cutting a quill:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument; vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort; mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz; puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere; puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit; fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	at the top of the instrument is a spout, so that when you tilt it, the liquid flows out; therefore empty half or one-third of it, for if you empty more than is appropriate in that hour, the patient may die from the shock to his spirit due to the instrument, or he may faint, or he will be close to death; but empty according to the quantity of his strength and according to what the dispositions of his strength signify, and his pulses; then withdraw the instrument and retain the liquid, which is now retained by the stopper that blocks the hole in the syphac, about which I have spoken, and which you should pierce according to this method; then reinsert the instrument the next day if you see the patient can endure it, and draw out a small quantity of liquid; do this every day, and beware of overdoing it as long as some liquid remains.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre; et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	If you have doubts about the illness, leave it with a lot of water, and treat it with hot sand or ash, and with much sweating or bathing and in the sun, and if it changes color from drinking; and treat it with medicines that dry up wounds until it is healed, and cauterize the stomach and liver and spleen after the extraction of the fluid, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	of the stoppage of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without a foreskin, or with a small foreskin, or with it in the wrong place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If necessary, pierce it immediately with a very thin and sharp spike according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet; et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	Then put in the foreskin a subtle plug of lead, and tie it, and leave it thus for 3 or 4 days, and when he wants to urinate, remove the plug, and he will urinate, and then replace it; and perhaps it is not necessary at all, because the fluid that comes out pushes the foreskin open.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	Those whose opening is small, if they are medicated with the plaster of lead white, as we have said, will open up.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut; et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	Those who do not have the opening in their place are bloated, for some are born with the opening at the head of the penis, which prevents them from urinating before they lift their penis upwards; and they cannot ejaculate because the matter cannot reach the urethra, and this is a serious illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient; et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the way to treat it is for the patient to lie on his back, then the head and shaft of the penis are pulled up like a feather, as far as it will go; and take care to prevent bleeding which often occurs, and if it does happen, then stop the flow with that which stops blood flow, and cure the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	of pustules on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide; et en i a malignes et non malignes; si covient que tu les preignes a .i. oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien; puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Many times these whitlows come on the penis, and it is an ugly appearance of flesh; and there are harmful and harmless ones; therefore you should squeeze them gently with a pair of tweezers, and pull out the roots, then clean and dry them, then apply cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment; then cure it with тонконгоном until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the ulcer is malignant, putrid and discolored, then you must apply cautery.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier; et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	When you have cut it, and if the ulcer is on the shaft of the penis, and part of it is inside and part outside, then you must first remove the ulcer that is inside; and when it is healed, treat the one outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion; si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Because when you treat it together, if the glans of the penis is not protected so that it is not pierced, and blackness and corruption come to it in its glans and scrotum; then cut off all that is black and corrupted, then bind on the ointment of honey and flour made from pomegranate rinds and walnuts, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if there is bleeding, administer the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble: c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption; et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi; et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars; et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil; puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	The cauteries help in two ways together: that is, in bleeding and corruption; and if the glans of the penis is infected and drawn, then you must boil or conduct water through the shaft of the penis, and the patient must urinate among it; and when the foreskin is tight at the tip of the penis which happens to those who have not been circumcised, either due to a wound or an abscess, then you must cut it with an instrument, so that the membrane is loosened and the glans of the penis is freed from all sides; and if it is a painful thing to discuss this, then you should cut it with a spatula made of wood at the tip of the penis and around the foreskin; then open gently between them, and put a thin damp linen cloth in cold water over it so that it does not swell again.
de la circoncision	of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not dismemberment of continuation like the other wounds; nevertheless, when we do this work of our own will and properly on children, it is necessary for us to do the best work, and the lightest for salvation.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not tell of their children's circumcision because they did not use it in their law, and we have nothing on this subject except what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	For I have seen the greater part of masters and doctors who performed circumcision around the glans, and on strong ones, and on all a new foreskin; so the foreskin shrinks because there are two membranes, and by chance one grows above and the other below remains.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Then they heal, and the pain is doubled, and in the healing which is from the nail there is no certainty that the point of the member is healed; and in the healing of the nail sometimes the iron slips away, and they ruin the work, and many times they heal in such a way that they do not need to be healed, and I have seen it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the healing that is done with strength throughout all the thread of the wound I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the forces cut justly above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir; et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues; puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens; puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens; puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien; et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge; puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres; et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Because when you press your hand, you cut it evenly all around; but the thread must be tightly wound around the skin; and the method of the first operation is that you make the child think that you are only tying the thread around the wand, and then you make him pull it in every way you can; then you hold it straight between your hands, and press your fingers or the soles of your feet against your hands so that the child does not see them, nor any of the instruments; then put your hand to the wand and breathe on the wound, and draw it up so that the head of the wand is in; then clean it well from the filth that has gathered there, then tie the place with a double thread, and then tie it under the other end; and hold it by both ends by the second ligature to the pouch and the index finger, and press between the two threads, then lift the wound gently and draw out the head of the wand; then let the blood run little by little, for that is the wound; and put powder on top of the powder a cloth glued with an egg cooked in rosewater, confited with good fresh rosemary oil, and leave it on until the next day, and treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The form of the force for purification is as follows: the two knees should be relaxed and straight, and the hands should be as large as the forearm equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision; donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme; et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	The error of purification is when the wound inside bleeds; therefore, you should stretch it with your fingernail, so that the blood makes an abscess; then, press it equally, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, hold it with tweezers, and then press.
Et s’il trespassent .iij. jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement; si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	And if it bleeds for three days, and what is under the skin is swollen, let it be until the abscess is healed and the wound slightly scarred; then press as much as you can, and beware of the part of the penis, it will not harm him in any way.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point; cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Thus treat the site of sudden wounds with powder, as we said in the treatise on powders, and if it bleeds profusely and goes above, it will do no harm; therefore treat it, as we said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	retaining urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division; et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e; et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	The retenetion of urine is due to a stone, or frozen blood, or bowels, or Char nee, or similar things that we have mentioned in the division; and if the urine is not released, and you see the retenetion is caused by the stone which is lodged at the neck of the bladder, then the patient should bend forward onto his knees; and his feet should be placed on his back, and he should stretch his abdomen from above the back, and hold himself in that position as much as he can; and thus the neck of the bladder is forced upwards to expel the stone, which will release the urine. If it does not come out as we have described, and the patient feels great pain, then you should administer extraction using an instrument called a "syringe", of which this is the form: it should be made of thin silver, as light as a bird's feather; its tube should be half a palm long, and thin at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede; puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine; et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And the way to release the urine is that you take a double thread and tie it to the tip of some wool or cotton, and insert the tip of the thread into the syringe; and squeeze out the excess wool and push it all the way to the tip of the syringe, then grease the syringe with oil or butter and egg white, and have the patient sit on a chair, and lubricate his penis with moist oil and olive oil and warm water; then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the body; then fill the syringe all the way to the bladder, and feel the patient's bladder being emptied, and if this is not done in this order, it will be because the person guiding it has done it incorrectly; then pull out the thread through the wool, and let the urine flow along the wool, then remove the thread, and release the urine; and repeat with the syringe until the bladder is empty and the patient feels relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	of diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When blood or scabs appear in the bladder, and pus has gathered there, and you see water and medicine dripping, then use all the apparatus called a “clepsydra”, and that is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus: II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est; et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira; et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	It is closed and has three openings: two on one side and one on the other, as you see; and the hair-like vessels through which the medicine reaches the penis are such that it blocks the penis without addition, so that if moisture can be drawn out and pushed in when necessary; and when you see your medicines leaking into the bladder, place the tip of the catheter into the moisture and draw it along the tract that is there; then you will draw the moisture to the catheter, and then push the tract inside firmly; then the moisture will enter inside, and will reach the bladder immediately, so that the patient feels it; and this is the form of the subtle catheter with which one catheters the bladder: thus it is.
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie; et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And it is made of silver or bronze, and the head is highest; and below there is one testicle or two; then take a bladder of a lamb and put the moisture that you see fit to catheterize the bladder, then tie it between the two testicles formed from a thin double thread, and heat this moisture over fire; then insert the tip of the catheter into the penis, then press your hand on the bladder gently until all the moisture enters, so that the patient feels that the moisture has reached the bladder; and if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment and make it into a circle, and pierce it all around with a needle; then insert the thread tightly into these openings, then assemble the circle as one assembles a ball, and put inside what you want of oil and moisture and water, and tie it in the instrument; and do as you did with the bladder, by pressing with your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	of stones
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	We have already discussed in the division the methods of stones, and their extraction along with medicines; and I have described the difference between stones formed in the kidneys, and all the signs, and on which type of stone one should operate by cutting; and in the bladder, and in the penis; and I will explain it clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	I say that the stone which is formed in the bladder occurs more frequently in children, and it is a sign that the water flows from the bladder similar to water in its subtlety; and it appears as a vein, and the patient feels pain in his penis, and he can urinate many times, and then it swells; and most of these have stones at the bottom; and the treatment is easier for those who have large stones than for those with small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient with an enema, in order to draw out all the feces which are in the bowels.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes clogs up the search for stones.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche dedens; se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	Then take the patient by the feet, and lift him up and move him around, so that the stone descends into the bladder, and sometimes comes out from above; then let him sit between your hands, and his hands be underneath his thighs, so that the bladder is completely tilted downward; then probe and touch inside; if you feel a stone in the space, then hurry now to cut into it.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	And if it does not come out with the touch, then moisten your index finger of your left hand with oil, if the patient is old, or your middle finger, if the patient is a young man; and insert it into his anus, and probe for the stone, and when you feel it at your finger, draw it toward the neck of the bladder; then press with your finger, and push it out to where you plan to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And instruct the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and instruct the patient to extend his testicles upwards in his right hand, and with his left hand pull back the skin under the testicles in the area where the incision is made; then insert the spatulum tightly, following its natural shape.
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans; par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And they make it between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the side of the left buttock; and let him be straight on the stone, and his toes be on the anus, and let the incision be diagonal so that it is wide at the top and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large; sometimes it presses the toe which is on the anus, so that it jumps out without effort; and know that there is a kind of stone with angles and edges: it is difficult to remove. And there is a kind that is underneath, similar to a gland, round, whose output is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole; et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	And for those with angles and edges, make the incision larger; and if it does not jump out, you must pull it with tweezers which are like a file at the tip, to extract the stone so that it does not escape; or you insert an instrument under it, with a curved tip. And if you cannot grip it in this way, then enlarge the opening, and if the blood vessels rupture, then constrict with vitriol; and if there is more than one stone, then first insert the largest at the neck of the bladder, then push up from below, then pull the rest out, and the smaller ones after.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it must be sewn up, and a larger wound made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces; et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	For two things happen to the patient: either they die or their urine comes out through the wound that cannot heal; but nevertheless, try to pull it with forceps until you have torn it in pieces; and when you have finished your work, smear the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, and constrict it, and place over it a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rosewater and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess; then re-bind the patient's neck, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, then wash the area very well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment, until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit; puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And if hot abscesses and corrosions come in the wound, and congealing of blood in the bladder, and the urine is retained because of it, which happens in such a way that there is pain with the urination: then thrust your finger into the wound and draw out that blood, for if it remains there, it will corrupt the bladder and burst; then wash the wound with water and vinegar and salt, and help him in every way you know until he is healed; and it is necessary that whenever you treat it, to bind his two thighs together, and assemble the remedies over the affected area.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	And if the stone is small and lodged in the urethra, causing it to be blocked, and the urine cannot pass; then the treatment of what I have said before serves as an excuse for cutting, and one should cut many times through this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already proven this.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	And if it is the size of a walnut or an egg, and it is in the entrance to the stomach, so that it cannot pass through the passage; take a piece of iron according to this shape and have 3 angles fixed on a stick:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	Then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone so that it cannot go back into the bladder; then insert the probe gently into the penis until it reaches the stone; and turn the probe in your hand inside the stone, little by little, until you pierce the stone from another side; then urine will come out at once, then press your hand on what is left of the stone that is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides; et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it is broken at once and comes out with the urine, then the patient is healed; but if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, then tie a thread under the stone and another above it, then pull the penis towards the stone between the two threads, then pull it out, and untie the string, and clean the congealed blood in the wound; and treat it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of female stones
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It sometimes happens that a stone becomes stuck in women, and if it does, the cure is painful, and it is forbidden for three reasons: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; and the second is that one cannot find a skilled woman who reveals herself to midwives, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere; et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And the third way is that by chance one cannot find a woman well skilled in this art of medicine; and the fourth way is that the stone of the woman is more embedded than the stone of a man, so it must be cut deeper, and there is greater fear involved. And if necessity demands it, one should take a midwife who is very skilled, and with difficulty she will find it, and if you cannot find one, then use a very subtle cast; and show her a wise dance in the life of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and command her to do what you command from the examination of the stone; and look very carefully to see if the woman is a virgin. Then she should push her finger into the urethra and seek the stone; and if she finds it, then she should press it under her finger, and recommend that she pushes her finger or thumb into the wound and wants and presses her left hand on the bladder firmly.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite; puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	If she finds it, she should move it from the bladder up to the root of the thigh; then press on the stone in the root of the thigh towards the middle of the hip, where the movement is felt, and feel for the stone in that area; do not move the finger above or below the stone, and make the incision small at first. Then enlarge the wound as much as needed so that you can feel the stone, and know that there are many types of stones: some are small and smooth, others large and rough, long and round, and some have a rainy texture.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	you will know their appearance to identify the exit point.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre; et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the blood flows, put powdered vitriol on the spot and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding stops; then return to your work and remove the stone with the tools I told you about earlier; have assistants to help you in this task. If the blood flows and it is from an artery that has been cut, apply the powder to the wound and press it firmly with bandages and a tourniquet; do not try to pull out the stone, as the patient may bleed to death; then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the swelling has gone down, return to your task until the stone is out.
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	Ramice aquouse is nothing other than the gathering of moisture or white pus, which is located under the membrane of the testicles, which holds the egg; and it is called "syfac", and sometimes it is properly in the membrane of the egg, if one believes that there is another egg; and this occurs when the skin of the testicle between the white pus that we have mentioned.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this ramice is due to weakness that comes to the testicles, and that matter is spread out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus; et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colors: or it is a yellowish color, or red, or black, or watery white, and so on; and these are the signs by which one can recognize this condition, for if it is in the white syphilis that we have mentioned, then the abscesses are like an egg, and there is no opening to the testicles, because there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef; et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if there is moisture in the skin itself, then the abscesses are like an egg with a part of an onion, and so one thinks it is another onion; and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white syphilis, then he feels good; therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, test all over the area where the shape is described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, then judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz; puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions; puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir; puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue; et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when we treat it with fire, the patient must be healed according to his strength and the fullness of his body; then he should lie on his back on something slightly raised, and have a lot of covering below him; then he should sit up on his left side, and direct the assistant to sit on his right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs of the heart; then take the spatulum gently, and cut the skin of the ribs among them in their length from above the nipple, and let the slit be straight while dividing the skin of the ribs up to the white skin, and peel it subtly according to his strength; then pierce the skin fully with water at a large hole, and draw out all the water, and then put your fingers in, and raise the skin upwards; and do not touch the heart itself, only the skin; cut everything equally in pieces, including the ribs, and do so subtly, or the water will return; if the wound jumps out of place during your work, reset it in its place when you have finished the work on the skin; then unite the two edges of the skin of the ribs with a single stitch, then cure it like other wounds until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the wound corrupted by another disease, then you should ligature the vessels that are suspended, fearing the flow of blood; then cut the skin all around the suspended area, extract the wound, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset; et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	And if the vein is divided into two parts together, know that they are two branches; then compress the other part as you did the first equally, then wash off the blood, and put in the wound soft lamb's wool moistened with rose oil; and put on another soft lamb's wool moistened with wine and oil, and put it over the two branches, and place doubled linen cloth on top, and tie it around all of the area which follows this pattern:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier; et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers; si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take two pieces of linen and stuff them with lamb's wool according to this appearance, and let them be sewn together at the crotch of the breeches, and one of the heads pressed against the anus to the back, and the other head over the perineum; and let the other two heads be on the two branches, and let all the binding be tied in the loop of the breeches; and sometimes this branch is treated with cautery instead of cutting with iron, and it is that you press a thin silver knife against the skin of the branches, and when the white pus containing the blood is revealed, take the knife according to this shape, and pierce that syphilis at the joints, and scorch it with this thin hot knife:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille; et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And cut in every way you can, as long as you remove everything; and be careful that the fire does not touch the egg; and know that this work is safer; and move, watching for blood flow, and changes in the incision; and if nothing contradicts you, whether an abscess or blood flow or anything else, then cure what contradicts you, according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit; pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer; puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee; et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this treatment due to its horror, then administer perforation as I have told you; and when you are certain through the signs that we have mentioned, that the pus is drained, then have the patient sit on a raised seat; then pierce the abscess at the bottom to the full breadth of the spatumile, and insert the perforation deep into the body; make the holes wide so that all the fluid can flow out; then place cotton over the wound and bandage it, and let the remaining fluid drain away, then treat the wound until it is healed; and if the white membrane does not allow the fluid to exit through the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used to treat hydrops, of which the shape has been described earlier; open the wound wider, and know that the fluid will return and be reabsorbed after six months or so, and when it is reabsorbed as before, the patient will recover.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse; et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	Know that in the dissection of this nerve there are many dispositions of fear, because of which it seems better to leave it alone; and I will tell you about its operation and the appearances of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I therefore say that many abscesses come about in the body, especially in the testes; and this happens in many cases.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion; et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief; et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	This is to be known through the overflow of bile and phlegm, which are spread throughout the body, or through impact; and the color of the abscess follows the color of the body; and there is no pain, and it is a serious abscess; and sometimes there are painful, pierceable abscesses, with a pus-like color, and at other times it comes from an artery, or from the inflammation of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois; et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	When it is from an artery, it is known by the hot disposition of the abscess, when you press it with your fingers; and you must not touch it.Quant c’est par enfleure de voine, si est conus quant li voinses soun tans et gonfliez, ou si tu le vès a la figure de l’aposteme selonc la disposition de la voinne; et si tu le presseres, li voinses soun tendus.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars; et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	Those who are affected by inflammation of the vein are identified by their appearance and the sensation when touched with the fingers; one can then properly make an incision on this appearance and other similar ones; you should cut the surface of the testicles, then the egg will be on top, and the white string will come out from under the egg, freeing the suspensory ligament in all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope; et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	If the egg is already rotten with these new characters, then you should therefore cut the egg and slice it; and if there is air in the scrotum or in what is inside the vessels, then one must free all those tendons and cut them roundly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the swelling is in the rear location, then you must cup it all and extract the testicle, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is finished, then cover the wound with soft wool moistened in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait; et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	This is a swelling wrapped in a wrapper similar to an onion, with the softening of the testicles, and the patient suffers greatly when he urinates; and the cure for this disease is also good, as fearful as it is, and we will nevertheless tell you how to treat it according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment; puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples; puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief; puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues; puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions; car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz; si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	It is necessary for you to make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then tie the suspensory band of the testicles tightly with your fingers, around all the vessels near the penis, and stretch them firmly; then cut through the vessels with a sharp spatula, widely and straight across their path, so that they are exposed, and then scrape each side, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries in the temples; then insert a needle where there is a double thread, and tie it to the first place where the vein appeared, and then directly to the other end; then pull them gently according to the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted moisture; then treat the wound as with the others, where a bowstring may be inserted so that any vessel which is not tied off can be tied off; for this does no harm, and if all the vessels are tied off, it is necessary to pull on the testicles at all the vessels, so that the urethra does not lose its supply of blood due to the incision of the vessels, and they do not become dry and unable to heal.
de la routure dou syfac	from the rupture of the sinus
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions; et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses; et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement; et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	The cause of this hernia is either through the incision that leads to the scrotum, or from an extension on the abdomen in the area of the groins, causing the intestines to descend from this opening to one of the testicles; and this opening is located in the scrotum, or from its extension, and these two types of hernias arise from many causes: from a blow, or from jumping, or from straining, or from lifting a heavy load, and from similar actions. The sign that it is an extension of the scrotum is that it occurs gradually over a long time and does not happen suddenly; and the hernia is even all the way to the bottom, because the scrotum presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are that it is of the section of the syphilis, that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and there are various abscesses appearing beneath the skin, close to the surface, and this is due to the escape of the intestines and the body from the syphilis.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the intestines descend with the feces, and are held back, causing great pain to the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these treatments of iron, there is fear, because of which one should abstain.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir; puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes; puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc; puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir; puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars; puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille; et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;
